@STX
I tried to guide the shapes to a corner where less strars will hit them. it was the upper left.
I added the growth so that the shapes duplicate and I will have more shapes. For the speed, I put it as high as posible since the beginning to finish with high speeds.
The shapes are spinning clockwise to grow.
At the end, I stopped the growth to keep the high number of shapes I already generated and stop the stars from appearing, so that they dont hit the shapes
At the final stage, I guided the shapes to a safe place, because the environment is harmful and the stars were approaching the corner, and are not expected to move to the lower side of the corner whent they hit the upper wall.
